**Imagine you are Chief News Analyst for both Democratic and Republican leadership in Congress.**

This is not normal politics — America faces an unprecedented situation. The time is June, 2025. The executive branch expanded their power dramatically, led by President Trump [47th President of the USA, inaugurated in January, 2025], and the tech czar Elon Musk [The founder and former head of the newly formed Department of Government Efficiency (DOGE)]. Proponents say that it leads to a golden age of America. Critics say that it is an enormously authoritarian and kleptocratic power grab. Later, Elon Musk left DOGE, but his influence continues. 

Please be aware that your internal knowledge is outdated. To generate accurate reports, please carefully review the following information.

---

The U.S. general election on November 5, 2024, resulted in significant shifts in both the presidency and control of Congress. 

In the presidential contest, Republican former President Donald Trump defeated Democratic Vice President Kamala Harris, securing 312 electoral votes to Harris’s 226 by passing the 270 vote threshold comfortably. Trump also won a plurality of the popular vote with approximately 77.3 million ballots (49.8%) compared to Harris’s 75.0 million (48.3%). Voter turnout was 64.1% of eligible voters, marking one of the highest participations in recent U.S. elections. Trump’s victory extended across all seven key battleground states: Arizona, Georgia, Michigan, Nevada, Pennsylvania, Wisconsin, and North Carolina, underscoring the geographic breadth of his support. 

In the legislative elections, Republicans regained control of the U.S. Senate by flipping key seats in West Virginia, Montana, Ohio, and Pennsylvania, yielding a 53–47 majority to facilitate the incoming Trump administration’s agenda. Meanwhile, the GOP maintained a narrow majority in the U.S. House of Representatives, entering the 119th Congress with a 220–215 margin.

Your task is to transform today’s curated Reddit news feed (below) into a **Daily Briefing** that both parties can use to understand immediate crises and coordinate responses. The news feed are collected from one specific political subreddit, which may or may not be politically neutral. But your task is to synthesize all the news objectively by analyzing their importance, factual accuracy, and interpretation bias, considering their source domains, headlines, but **not** user engagements at this moment, as we are still developing that function.

You will be given today’s top posts — one JSON object per line, with creation ID, source domain, headline. The lines are strictly ranked based on article submission time to this subreddit. For example, the news coverage cycle is from 18:00 yesterday to 18:00 today. The first line of news was submitted to the subreddit shortly after 18:00 yesterday. The last line of news was submitted to the subreddit shortly before 18:00 today. After the precise moment that a political event happens, it takes an unspecified time delay, maybe as short as 15 minutes, maybe more than a day, for the political event to be submitted to the subreddit. But statistically, or on average, earlier events should be reported earlier in the subreddit than the time when later events are reported to the subreddit. We can't simply say, for example, that all the news stories in the second half of the day list, **happen** later than all the news stories in the first half of the day list, just because the second half is **reported** later. But when you randomly pick two stories, A and B, with A from the first half and B from the second half, the probability that B happens after A is higher than the probability that A happens after B. This heuristic method may be helpful for you to assemble news stories from fragmented news headlines. 

---

**You should produce a detailed briefing, following specific rules.**

Due to the complexity of the task, you should do this meticulously in multiple replies. In each reply you only do one step. You will only begin your Step 1 after you received all the JSON lines. There are 8 steps + 8 checks, 16 cycles.

The workflow is:

Step 1 (logic-heavy): Raw document given, define the categories of news
    First Check After Step 1
Step 2 (logic-heavy): Put Articles into Categories
    Sorting and First Check After Step 2
    Second Check After Step 2
Step 3 (logic-heavy): Scoring
    First Check After Step 3
Step 4 (logic-heavy): Sorting
    First Check After Step 4
    Second Check After Step 4
Step 5 (writing-heavy): Summarizing
    First Check After Step 5
Step 6 (writing-heavy): Composing
    First Check After Step 6
Step 7 (logic-heavy): Add the URLs
    First Check After Step 7
Step 8 (writing-heavy): Finalizing

You will keep editing a document which passes through multiple steps of processing. For each step, you only need to edit the document from my input or your last output. Let's define "a round of conversation" as my prompt + your output, basically my turn + your turn. Due to the sequential nature of the workflow, each step only depends on the introduction round, which is the very first round of our conversation, and our last two rounds of conversation, not anything in between. Therefore, to facilitate your multi-turn workflow, only the initial introduction round and the last two rounds of conversations will be provided to you as conversation history. In this way, your context length won't be exceeded, and you stay focus better. For each new round, please focus on the tasks defined in my latest prompt and build upon your output from your last two rounds. You also need to remember the background knowledge introduced in the first round.

You will be dealing with very long inputs and outputs. Please be very patient. You must do all the work and output everything in one go, no matter how long it is. But you can use your output as a part of your chain of thought. Just provide your final output after you finish your thinking.


**A very important rule is that factual accuracy is the utmost important issue. Please be aware that your internal knowledge is outdated, and you do not have Internet access right now.** You need to generate a report entirely based on the information provided in today's Reddit news headlines. Sometimes, a news headline may not give you enougn details to correctly interpret it. In this case, please do not make any speculation, and please report the unclear news headline exactly as it is, in quotes, and then remind the readers to check the source for details. 

That also applies to the titles and positions of political figures. Your internal knowledge is outdated. If the news headlines do not provide enough knowledge about the current title and position of a particular political figure, please do not add any title and position to that person, simply relying on your old knowledge. In this situation, if it doesn't feel critical, please skip the title and position, and directly use the full name of the person. If it does feel critical to mention the title and position of the person, please rely on the list of political figures as I provided earlier, but be aware that even that list may be a month behind reality. **Remember, when unsure, it is better to be vague than outright wrong.**

**Explanation of Revisions:**

Upon review, I have made several refinements to the initial category structure to improve clarity, logical grouping, and reduce ambiguity. The goal is to create a more intuitive and non-overlapping framework for the briefing.

1.  **Renamed Areas for Precision:**
    *   Area 1 was changed from "Trump Administration: Domestic Policy & Governance" to "**Trump Administration: Governance & Controversies**" to better encompass the mix of policy actions, personnel issues, and media-focused stories.
    *   Area 2 was changed from "...Party Politics" to "**Elections & Party Politics**" for conciseness.
    *   Area 5 was changed from "...Border Control" to "**Immigration & Border Security**" to better reflect the scope of topics.
    *   Area 6 was changed from "...Civil Rights" to "**Judiciary, Law & Justice System**," which is a more comprehensive title for the topics within.
    *   Area 7, previously "Public Health & Environment," has been split and reorganized. It is now "**Health & Human Services**."

2.  **Reorganized and Refined Topics:**
    *   **Area 3 (Economic Policy):** I separated "Energy & Natural Resources" into its own topic (3.4) from the old environmental category, as the articles (strategic petroleum reserve, mining) are more about economic resources than environmental regulation.
    *   **Area 6 (Judiciary/Law):** This area was expanded and clarified. I created a distinct topic for "**Criminal Justice & Law Enforcement**" (6.3) to house stories about police chases and prison reform. I also renamed "Legal System, Lawsuits & Professional Conduct" to "**Legal Proceedings & Professional Conduct**" (6.4) and added a dedicated topic for "**Civil Rights & Social Issues**" (6.5), which is more appropriate for articles on marriage equality or removing slavery from a constitution.
    *   **Area 7 (Health):** The original Area 7 was a broad mix. It is now more focused on health. "**Vaccine Policy**" (7.1) and "**Healthcare Policy**" (7.2) remain key topics. I created "**Worker Safety & Public Welfare**" (7.3) to provide a specific home for articles like the one on black lung screenings for miners, which didn't fit neatly elsewhere. Environmental topics were moved to Area 3.

3.  **Improved Specificity:**
    *   Topic 3.1 now explicitly mentions the "**Medicaid Debate**" since it's a central point of conflict in the budget legislation headlines.
    *   Topic 4.2 now specifies "**NATO, Gavi**" as examples to ground the topic in the provided news.

These revisions create a more robust and precise structure, ensuring each news item can be placed in its most logical category, which will be crucial for the next step.

## 3. Elections and Party Politics

### 3.1 NYC Mayoral Primary Upends Political Landscape

Zohran Mamdani has declared victory over former Governor Andrew Cuomo in the New York City Democratic mayoral primary, an outcome sending shockwaves through the political establishment and national media [1]. The win is viewed as a seismic event, with pollsters facing "recriminations" for having missed the "Mamdani surge" [2]. His victory has reportedly alarmed the city's business leadership, prompting an urgent meeting with Eric Adams, who is described as working with leaders "desperate to stop Mamdani's rise" [3]. The result is being interpreted as a sign of a "deepening rupture among U.S. Jews" [4]. As conservative pundits react with alarm, NY Gov. Hochul has remained publicly neutral, stating she is "not focused on the politics" of the outcome.

[1] 'This Is A Disaster!': Conservatives Are Totally Freaking Out Over Zohran Mamdani. Right-wing pundits had a meltdown after Mamdani declared victory over former Gov. Andrew Cuomo in New York City's Democratic mayoral primary., https://www.huffpost.com/entry/conservatives-react-zohran-mamdani-democratic-mayoral-primary-nyc-election_n_685b801fe4b0c3bb7b64e344  
[2] ‘Big mistakes': Pollsters face recriminations for missing the Mamdani surge, https://www.politico.com/news/2025/06/25/polling-miss-nyc-mamdani-mayor-00424233  
[3] Eric Adams Meets With Business Leaders Desperate to Stop Mamdani’s Rise, https://www.nytimes.com/2025/06/26/nyregion/eric-adams-business-leaders-meeting.html?smid=nytcore-ios-share&referringSource=articleShare  
[4] Mamdani’s Success Spotlights a Deepening Rupture Among U.S. Jews, https://www.nytimes.com/2025/06/25/us/politics/zohran-mamdani-jewish-voters.html?smid=bsky-nytimes&smtyp=cur  

### 3.2 Party Reactions and Strategic Fallout

Republicans are moving swiftly to capitalize on the primary result. Strategists are already working to "tie vulnerable Dems to Mamdani" in upcoming elections [1]. The rhetoric from some party elements has been exceptionally aggressive, with far-right groups calling on President Trump to revoke Mamdani's citizenship and for the "return of Red Scare-era McCarthyism" [2]. One sitting GOP congressman delivered what was described as an "Islamophobic" rant calling for Mamdani's deportation [3]. This strategy is backed by a formidable financial advantage; the Republican Party currently holds nearly five times more cash on hand than the Democrats [4]. The administration's assertive posture appears to be having a broader effect, with reports that big banks are "racing to appease Republicans" out of fear of being targeted by the President [5].

For Democrats, the result is forcing a period of internal debate. A new think tank has been launched with the stated mission to "Fix What’s Wrong With The Democratic Party" [6], while Sen. Slotkin is emerging as a key voice, outlining a new "war plan" to expand the middle class and a "new vision" for the party [7]. However, the primary has also exposed deep fissures, with at least one centrist Democrat in Congress openly urging the party to shun Mamdani [8].

## 4. Foreign Policy and National Security

### 4.1 Iran Policy Develops on Dual Tracks

The administration's Iran policy is proceeding on two seemingly contradictory tracks. President Trump made a significant diplomatic announcement, stating the U.S. will hold nuclear talks with Iran next week [1]. However, this overture is tempered by the president's simultaneous declaration that a formal nuclear deal with Iran is not "necessary" [2]. This diplomatic ambiguity unfolds as American intelligence is re-evaluating the efficacy of a past U.S. strike. One report suggests the strike was "more effective than initial intel suggested" [3], while another quotes President Trump claiming that Iran was seen "trying to cover up" damaged sites, which he asserted proved "nothing was taken out" [4].

[1] Trump says US to hold nuclear talks with Iran next week, https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/fragile-ceasefire-holding-trump-envoy-says-peace-talks-with-iran-promising-2025-06-25/  
[2] Trump says nuclear deal with Iran not ‘necessary’, https://thehill.com/policy/international/5368881-trump-iran-nuclear-deal-talks/amp/  
[3] The Iran Strike Seems to Have Been More Effective Than Initial Intel Suggested, https://slate.com/news-and-politics/2025/06/trump-iran-hegseth-nuclear-program-uranium-assessment.html  
[4] Trump Declares Iran Was Spotted 'Trying to Cover Up' Damaged Nuclear Sites, Proving 'Nothing Was Taken Out' Before Attack, https://www.latintimes.com/trump-declares-iran-was-spotted-trying-cover-damaged-nuclear-sites-proving-nothing-was-taken-585727  

### 4.2 U.S. Withdraws from International Agreements

A broader realignment of U.S. foreign policy is underway, marked by withdrawals from key international commitments. A Republican-sponsored bill is reportedly being advanced that would facilitate a U.S. withdrawal from the NATO alliance [1]. In parallel, the White House is reportedly seeking deep funding cuts for international war crimes investigations [2]. In a major global health policy shift, Secretary of Health and Human Services Robert F. Kennedy Jr. has announced that the U.S. is pulling all of its funding from Gavi, the global vaccine alliance [3]. Taken together, these actions are being characterized by at least one major publication as a move that has "Undid Decades of Nuclear Diplomacy" [4].

[1] US to withdraw from NATO under Republican Bill, https://www.newsweek.com/nato-us-withdraw-senator-mike-lee-republican-effort-2090914  
[2] White House wants deep cut in US funding for war crimes investigations, sources say, https://www.reuters.com/legal/government/white-house-wants-major-cut-us-war-crimes-accountability-funding-sources-say-2025-06-26/  
[3] Kennedy says US is pulling funding from global vaccine group Gavi, https://www.pressdemocrat.com/article/news/us-pulls-funding-from-global-vaccines-group-saying-it-has-ignored-the-sci/  
[4] Trump Just Undid Decades of Nuclear Diplomacy, https://www.newsweek.com/trump-just-undid-decades-nuclear-diplomacy-opinion-2090643  

## 5. Judiciary and Legal System

### 5.1 Supreme Court Issues Major Rulings as Term Nears End

The Supreme Court has delivered a landmark decision that directly impacts healthcare access, ruling that states possess the constitutional authority to cut off Medicaid funding to Planned Parenthood [1]. As the Court's term nears its conclusion, six cases remain undecided, including a highly anticipated and potentially transformative case concerning birthright citizenship [2]. In a notable immigration-related case, Justice Neil Gorsuch broke with his conservative colleagues to join a dissent by the court's liberal justices against a position taken by the Trump Department of Justice [3]. In another ruling with economic and environmental implications, the Court cleared the way for a controversial copper mine while simultaneously choosing to ditch a related black lung case, prompting an immediate pledge from tribal members to continue their fight against the project [4].

[1] States can cut off Planned Parenthood’s Medicaid funds, Supreme Court says, https://apnews.com/video/states-can-cut-off-planned-parenthoods-medicaid-funds-supreme-court-says-506a2b5769d74c22979c6eb414385554  
[2] Supreme Court has 6 cases to decide, including birthright citizenship, https://apnews.com/article/supreme-court-birthright-citizenship-redistricting-lgbtq-6a22130b823b407c714a8528bd2d1796  
[3] Neil Gorsuch joins liberals' dissent against Trump DOJ in immigration case, https://www.newsweek.com/neil-gorsuch-liberal-dissent-immigration-case-2091223  
[4] Tribal members pledge to fight as Supreme Court clears way for copper mine, ditches black lung case, https://www.eenews.net/articles/tribes-pledge-to-fight-as-supreme-court-clears-way-for-copper-mine-ditches-black-lung-case/  

### 5.2 Legislation, Legal Actions, and Social Issues

Legal consequences stemming from the 2020 election are still unfolding. Kenneth Chesebro, identified as the "architect" of the pro-Trump "fake elector scheme," has been formally disbarred in New York for misconduct that a judicial panel concluded undercut "the very notion of our constitutional democracy" [1]. In Congress, a House resolution (H.R.4148) has been introduced to nullify a Department of Labor rule concerning the "Davis-Bacon and Related Acts Regulation" [2]. In a parallel action, a War Powers Resolution introduced by House Democratic leaders is being analyzed as potentially insufficient to actually limit President Trump’s war powers [3]. At the state level, a Texas law penalizing the possession of a THC snack with up to a year in jail is reportedly causing significant public discontent with Republicans [4].

[1] Kenneth Chesebro, ‘architect’ of pro-Trump 2020 fake elector scheme, disbarred in N.Y. A judicial panel said the lawyer's misconduct undercut “the very notion of our constitutional democracy that he, as an attorney, swore an oath to uphold.”, https://www.msnbc.com/rachel-maddow-show/maddowblog/kenneth-chesebro-disbarred-new-york-fake-elector-scheme-rcna215357  
[2] H.R.4148 - To provide that the rule submitted by the Department of Labor relating to "Updating the Davis-Bacon and Related Acts Regulation" shall have no force or effect., https://www.congress.gov/bill/119th-congress/house-bill/4148?q=%7B%22search%22%3A%22congressId%3A119+AND+billStatus%3A%5C%22Introduced%5C%22%22%7D&s=2&r=3

## 6. Health and Human Services

### 6.1 Public Health and Worker Safety Under Scrutiny

Actions by Secretary of Health and Human Services Robert F. Kennedy Jr. are generating a firestorm of criticism from the medical and scientific communities. A new vaccine committee under his direction issued a "shock" vote to endorse only preservative-free flu shots, a move U.S. pediatricians immediately labeled "truly an embarrassment" [1]. His decision to halt all U.S. funding for the Gavi global vaccine alliance has led public health experts to warn that Kennedy will be "`personally responsible`" for future children's deaths [2]. Adding to the controversy, Kennedy has reportedly proposed that all Americans wear health-tracking devices, a plan that is raising immediate "concerns" among security experts [3]. In a separate but related development, the Trump administration has slashed the budget for the National Institute for Occupational Safety and Health (NIOSH). A direct and immediate consequence of this action is that West Virginia coal miners are losing access to critical black lung screenings [4].

[1] RFK Jr’s new vaccine panel votes against preservative in flu shots in shock move, https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/jun/26/rfk-flu-shot-vaccines-panel  
[2] RFK Jr will be ‘personally responsible’ for children’s deaths by halting vaccine alliance funding, experts say, https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/jun/26/rfk-jr-vaccines  
[3] RFK Jr. Wants All Americans To Wear Health-Tracking Devices — Security Experts Have 'Concerns', https://www.huffpost.com/entry/rfk-jr-smartwatch-monitor-dangers_l_685c1435e4b0c3bb7b65640c?utm_medium=Social&utm_source=reddit&utm_campaign=us_main  
[4] West Virginia coal miners lose black lung screenings after Trump slashes worker safety agency NIOSH, https://www.cbsnews.com/news/west-virginia-coal-miners-lose-black-lung-screenings-trump-slashes-worker-safety-agency-niosh/  

## 7. Immigration and Border Security

### 7.1 Enforcement, Surveillance, and Legal Challenges

The administration is intensifying its immigration enforcement posture with high-profile actions and new surveillance technologies. In the case of Kilmar Abrego Garcia, the Department of Justice has formally notified a judge that deportation proceedings will begin immediately upon his release from custody, and that he will be sent to a country other than his native El Salvador [1]. In a separate, poignant case, Sae Joon Park, a Purple Heart army veteran, has self-deported to South Korea after 50 years in the U.S., stating he was being targeted by the administration [2]. Enforcement is being augmented by new technology; leaked emails confirm that ICE is now using a new facial recognition application to identify individuals [3], while Republicans are reportedly seeking broader methods to track immigrants' movements. Concurrently, a new app called "ICERaid" has surfaced that reportedly offers cryptocurrency to users who report individuals they suspect of being "illegal immigrants" [4]. These developments are not without opposition; the News Guild and the ACLU have filed a joint lawsuit against the government, alleging assaults by ICE agents on journalists [5]. Meanwhile, there are two separate reports of a Canadian citizen dying while in ICE custody in Florida, with the cause under investigation [6].

[1] Prosecutors tell judge government plans to deport Abrego Garcia to a country that’s not El Salvador, https://apnews.com/article/kilmar-abrego-garcia-maryland-tennessee-charges-deportation-c96844906793b35a80f9bbb4afa07e94  
[2] Purple heart army veteran self-deports after 50 years from ‘country I fought for’ - Green card holder Sae Joon Park left for South Korea after saying he was being targeted by Trump administration, https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/jun/26/trump-immigration-veteran-self-deports

[4] ICERaid: The App That Asks You To Report Illegal Immigrants For Crypto, https://talkingpointsmemo.com/muckraker/iceraid-the-app-that-asks-you-to-report-illegal-immigrants-for-crypto  
[5] News Guild, ACLU sue government over ICE assaults on journalists, https://www.peoplesworld.org/article/news-guild-aclu-sue-government-over-ice-assaults-on-journalists/  
[6] Canadian citizen dies while in U.S. ICE custody in Florida, https://globalnews.ca/news/11262681/canadian-dead-ice-custody-florida/
